[30;1m36 | [0m[35mclass PageRange(object):[0m
[30;1m37 | [0m[35m    """[0m
[30;1m38 | [0m[35m    A slice-like representation of a range of page indices,[0m
[30;1m39 | [0m[35m        i.e. page numbers, only starting at zero.[0m
[30;1m40 | [0m[35m    The syntax is like what you would put between brackets [ ].[0m
[30;1m41 | [0m[35m    The slice is one of the few Python types that can't be subclassed,[0m
